## Current Status

Loans / Equity / Opening / Historical design checkpoint on 2026-07-01: `/finance-accounting/loan-contracts`, `/finance-accounting/loan-dashboard`, `/finance-accounting/equity-maint`, `/finance-accounting/opening-balance`, and `/finance-accounting/historical-data` now follow the active finance/accounting table baseline more closely. The Loan Contracts desktop table, Loan Dashboard upcoming/overdue due tables, Opening Balance accounts table, and Historical Data dynamic month table now use lined desktop table shells with `min-w-full divide-y divide-slate-200 text-sm`, `ResizableTableHead`, persisted resizable column widths, reset-width controls, Thai-first business headers, and safer numeric nowrap/tabular alignment. The Equity page has no desktop table in this read baseline, so its existing card/form layout remains in place. Existing KPI cards, tabs, disabled write/import actions, and mobile card views remain in place. This is a UI/layout cleanup only; no `/api/finance-accounting/loan-contracts`, `/loan-dashboard`, `/equity-maint`, `/opening-balance`, `/historical-data`, loan schedule/payment generation, equity save, opening balance apply/lock, historical clear/save/sync, GL, period close, bank, asset, stock, AP/AR, or business behavior changed. Validation passed: targeted ESLint for `LoansEquityPageClients.tsx`, `npm run lint --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next` (0 errors, existing unrelated warnings only), `npm run type-check --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next -- --pretty false`, and `npm run build --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`. Browser QA remains pending because this checkpoint covers local code/layout validation only.

NSERP-125 Receipt Voucher print follow-up on 2026-07-01: account selection now persists the selected supplier bank account instead of forcing `payment_method = รับเงินสด` on save. The print template uses that persisted selected account only for the `เลขที่บัญชี / Bank Account` box, and falls back to the supplier's first active bank account for older RV records where the selected account was previously lost. The document header and green total summary remain `รับเงินสด` / `ยอดรับเงินสด` to match the user mockup. This fixes the case where the form visually selected a bank account but the printed RV still showed the amount-in-words box.

WTO durable read-model optimization checkpoint on 2026-06-30: removed remaining sales-side WTO read paths that parsed `sales_bills.items` JSON for usage. `apps/next/src/lib/server/weight-tickets.ts` now reads active sales usage and downstream bill references from `sales_bill_source_allocations` (with bill-status guard) while timeline history continues to read `weight_ticket_usage_logs`. `/api/daily/weight-tickets` list no longer does one usage query per row; it batch-loads purchase/sales usage counts by `weight_ticket_id`, eliminating the N+1 pattern on the list page. `/api/sales/bills` WTO availability summary also now reads `sales_bill_source_allocations.meta.deliverySummaryId` instead of scanning bill item JSON. This batch changes read/query source only; WTO/SB write flow and business states are unchanged. Validation: `npm run type-check --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next -- --pretty false`.
Sales Bill detail no-fallback checkpoint on 2026-06-30: removed the remaining Sales Bill detail fallback that built bill items from `sales_bills.items` JSON snapshot when durable `sales_bill_lines` facts were missing. `getSalesBillDetail()` now requires durable line facts and source/allocation facts as the only read model. If an older or malformed SB has no durable facts, `/api/sales/bills/[id]` returns an explicit contract error instead of silently reconstructing detail from snapshot JSON. `readModelWarning` is no longer used for this fallback path. Validation: `npm run type-check --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next -- --pretty false`, `npm run build --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`.

Added pagination buttons at the bottom of the Desktop table list in Weight Ticket List. In Stock Operation, added client-side pagination (20 items per page) and top controls in Grade Adjustment (convert mode), and bottom controls for all modes (status-convert, adjust, convert) beneath the main table. Local type-checking, lint checks, and production build succeeded.
Product Tracking Annual Data (NSERP-132) checkpoint on 2026-06-30: Fixed a bug where the annual month-by-month compare table in Product Tracking (under the 'รายปี' tab) displayed empty data dashes ('-') for all products. The root cause was a key mismatch in the `/api/tracking/product` API endpoint: the accumulated monthly data map `productMonthlyMap` was populated using the numeric `product.id` (as a string) as the key, but the subsequent rows map retrieved it using `row.id` (which corresponds to `product.code`). Changed the map key during accumulation to `product.code` to resolve the mismatch. Local type-checking and Next.js production build verified successfully.

Removed the legacy "ผูก Supplier กับพนักงานขาย" section from the main page. Re-implemented the `/api/sales-commission` endpoint to accept query parameters `dateFrom`, `dateTo`, and `branchId`. Re-implemented `buildSalesCommission` in `main-sales-control.ts` to compute current period and annual totals, verify commission eligibility (salesperson `commission_eligible` is true, item price <= face price `sales_price`), and calculate commission using strict step tier rules (base >= 1M gives 1000, and +500 for each additional 500k strictly above). Re-implemented `SalesCommissionPageClient` component in `MainSalesControlClients.tsx` to feature: 1. Period and Branch filters; 2. 8 Summary Metrics Cards; 3. Salesperson Cards Grid; 4. "สรุปยอดซื้อราย Sales" pivot table by product category; and 5. Individual detail drilldown view featuring 4 verification tables with search, sort, and pagination. Validation: `npm run type-check` and `npm run build` both successfully passed.

The first supported correction slice mirrors Purchase Bill's allocation-edit pattern for changes that do not affect stock: line count, product, WTO source, and gross/deduct/net/qty must remain unchanged; users can change `Spot Sale <-> PO Sell`, price, discount, note, VAT/header totals, and export order. `PATCH /api/sales/bills` now rejects active RCP/customer-advance edits, marks old active `sales_bill_po_sell_allocations.status = reversed` (Sales Bill table allows `active/cancelled/reversed`, not PB-style `released`), creates new allocation rows, appends `po_sell_allocation_logs` release/allocate events, recalculates `po_sells.remaining_qty/remaining_amount/status`, and updates Sales Bill AR totals/balance without touching stock ledger or WTO pending_out. UI wording no longer says "ล็อกใบส่งของเดิม"; edit mode now says it keeps the original business identity for audit continuity. After create or edit save, the list must reload with the user's current search/filter/page context and must not auto-fill the search box with the saved SB doc no. Historical reporting snapshot checkpoint on 2026-06-24: user asked to cover History/Snapshot for old Bill, old PO, finance, stock, and other dashboard data that must roll up from daily to monthly/yearly. Added `docs/notes/Reporting History Snapshot Policy.md` as the cross-domain contract: separate transaction facts, document snapshots, and reporting snapshots; group business metrics by `business_date/document_date`; use `as_of_date` for historical views; derive monthly/yearly from checked daily snapshots; and never fallback from missing historical facts to current-state balances. User then clarified stock must support real-time and historical views for both quantity and WAC/ต้นทุนเฉลี่ย; stock docs now require quantity, value, WAC, pending_out, and available to be calculated with the same cutoff, with historical WAC derived from ledger value/qty as-of instead of current WAC. Sales Bill WTO return/loss checkpoint on 2026-06-25: the explicit `รับของคืน` action belongs on WTO detail, not Sales Bill detail. `/api/daily/weight-tickets/[id]/stock-returns` exposes active return candidates only when a WTO has already been allocated to an active SB and still has remaining `pending_out` after partial billing. The submit action still posts through `POST /api/sales/bills/{docNo}/stock-return` so the audit is linked to SB/WTO/product/warehouse. User must enter actual returned weight. Exact return releases the pending_out and decrements WTO remaining weight without writing stock ledger because that unsold qty was never stock-out in ledger. Short return requires a reason, splits/closes pending_out into returned + `lost`, appends `returned_from_sales_bill` and `loss_from_sales_bill` usage logs, and writes `stock_ledger.ref_type = WTO-RETURN-LOSS` for the loss qty/value using the current WAC of that stock bucket. Sales Bill detail remains a read-only bill detail surface for this action. Docs updated in Sales Bill flow, Stock Ledger DB/API design, Stock Ledger/Balance, and tasklist. Validation passed: `npm run type-check --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`, `npm run lint --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next` (existing tracking-page warnings only), and `git diff --check`.
Stock Sale pending_out hardening checkpoint on 2026-06-25: confirmed the durable Sales Bill allocation tables already exist and are written on new SB create/cancel (`sales_bill_lines`, `sales_bill_source_allocations`, `sales_bill_po_sell_allocations`, `sales_bill_customer_advance_allocations`). This batch did not add fallback paths. Runtime/service/API business names now use `pending_out`; `stock_holds` remains only the technical DB table name. Removed the old service compatibility alias names so type-check fails if a caller still uses the old concept. Stock Balance detail payload now exposes `pendingOutKey` and UI wording says pending_out. SB cancel after WTO return/loss now checks real return/loss usage facts and will not reopen pending_out or increment WTO remaining summary again; it only posts `SB-CANCEL` stock ledger for the sold qty.
Sales Bill export order checkpoint on 2026-06-25: added target field `sales_bills.export_order_no` for foreign sales bills via migration `20260625113000_add_sales_bill_export_order_no.sql`, applied to dev-target and marked in `supabase_migrations.schema_migrations`. The `/sales/bills` create modal now shows `เลขที่ order ส่งออก` immediately after the read-only `ช่องทางขาย` only when the selected Customer has `marketScope = ต่างประเทศ`. Client/API validation requires the field for foreign Customers and rejects it for domestic Customers; this is a new explicit column and does not reuse or fallback to `ref_no`. Detail and print surfaces show the export order number when present.
Sales Stock partial-billing checkpoint on 2026-06-24: updated `/sales/bills` Stock SB create flow so commercial sales quantity and stock consume quantity are separate. In the modal, `น้ำหนักสุทธิที่ส่ง` is the read-only WTO net after container deduction, `จำนวนที่ขายได้` is the Customer-side accepted/weighed quantity, `หักสิ่งเจือปน` is the Customer quality deduction, and `น้ำหนักขายสุทธิ = จำนวนที่ขายได้ - หักสิ่งเจือปน`. API validation now allows Customer accepted weight to be less than or greater than the WTO sent weight; stock consume is capped by the active WTO `pending_out` quantity and saved as `stockIssueQty` in Sales Bill snapshots/allocation metadata. `consumeActiveWtoPendingOut` now supports partial consume by reducing the active pending_out and creating a consumed pending_out slice for the SB, so remaining `pending_out` stays active for the required `รับของคืน` action on WTO detail. SB cancel can reopen consumed pending_out slices only before return/loss facts exist; after return/loss, cancel returns stock directly through `SB-CANCEL` and must not recreate pending_out.

AR/AP docs-first checkpoint on 2026-06-24: user asked to update documents before implementation. Updated the finance contracts so `/finance/ar` no longer mentions Pending Sale / stock issue summary, AR/AP rows must read visible balances from `sales_bills.receivable_balance` / `received_amount` and `purchase_bills.payable_balance` / `paid_amount`, and allocation/payment/receipt facts are drilldown-only. `/finance/ap` now explicitly has no channel filter until purchase channel exists as a real document source, and this implementation batch must not add credit-term/due-date schema; AP aging remains based on `purchase_bills.date`. Tasklist now tracks the remaining code work separately: AR API source-of-truth, AP API source-of-truth, AR/AP drilldown, AP channel filter removal, and AR/AP UI alignment with `docs/design.md` / Peach.
AR/AP balance-source checkpoint on 2026-06-24: user asked to record what affects AR/AP and how each page must calculate it. Target rule is now documented as one contract: AR is created only when `Sales Bill (SB)` is saved, reduced by active `RCP` and Customer Advance allocation, and read from `sales_bills.receivable_balance` / `sales_bills.received_amount`; `PO Sell` and `WTO` do not create AR. AP is created only when `Purchase Bill (PB)` is saved, reduced by active `PMT` and Supplier Advance allocation, and read from `purchase_bills.payable_balance` / `purchase_bills.paid_amount`; `POB`, `WTI`, and `PMA` do not create or reduce AP. Receipt/payment/allocation tables are drilldown/audit facts, not the primary balance source. Docs updated in Finance AR/AP page flows plus Sales/Purchase flows, and tasklist now tracks API follow-up for `/api/finance/ar` and `/api/finance/ap`.
AR/RCP source-of-truth checkpoint on 2026-06-24: user asked when AR is created and whether current AR is correct. Confirmed target rule: AR is created when `Sales Bill (SB)` is saved, not when `RCP` is saved; `RCP` only reduces AR. `WTO` does not create AR. For read/report surfaces, `sales_bills.receivable_balance` and `sales_bills.received_amount` must be the primary AR balance fields, while `customer_receipt_allocations`, `customer_receipts`, and legacy `receipts` are drilldown/audit facts. Current `/api/finance/ar` still aggregates legacy `receipts` into a received map before falling back to `sales_bills.received_amount`, which can overstate AR when Customer Advance was allocated at SB creation. Docs and tasklist updated; implementation follow-up is to change `/api/finance/ar` to read `sales_bills` balance snapshots first and add RCP/Customer Advance allocation drilldown without deriving balance from legacy receipt rows.
AP/PMT source-of-truth checkpoint on 2026-06-24: user asked whether AP has the same issue as AR. Confirmed target rule: AP is created when `Purchase Bill (PB)` is saved, not when `PMT` is saved; `PMT` only reduces AP. `WTI` does not create AP and `PMA` is approval/queue, not payment. For read/report surfaces, `purchase_bills.payable_balance` and `purchase_bills.paid_amount` must be the primary AP balance fields, while `payments`, `payment_allocations`, `payment_approvals`, and `supplier_advance_allocations` are drilldown/audit facts. Current `/api/finance/ap` still aggregates non-cancelled `payments` into a paid map before falling back to `purchase_bills.paid_amount`, which can overstate AP when Supplier Advance was allocated to PB. Docs/tasklist updated; implementation follow-up is to change `/api/finance/ap` to read `purchase_bills` balance snapshots first and add PMT/ADV allocation drilldown without deriving balance from payment rows.
WTO/SB return-cancel costing checkpoint on 2026-06-24: user confirmed the target rule for `WTO -> SB -> รับของคืน -> SB cancel`. If an SB is cancelled before any return-from-WTO/SB exists, cancellation may reopen the consumed `WTO pending_out` back to active. If return-from-WTO/SB already happened, cancellation must not reopen/recreate `pending_out`; the existing return/diff audit remains as posted, and `SB-CANCEL` returns stock directly for the SB-sold quantity using the original SB unit cost/value snapshot. Example: WTO sends 100, SB sells 50, actual return is 48 with diff/loss 2; later SB cancel returns 50 through `SB-CANCEL`, final stock restoration is 98 and diff/loss 2 stays as audit. Docs updated in Sales Bill flow, Sales flow, Stock Ledger design, Stock Balance design, WTI/WTO flow, and Sales Bill page-flow notes. Implementation follow-up: build the return-from-WTO/SB write path and make SB cancel branch on real return facts, with no fallback to PSALE or silent status inference.
Customer/Supplier branch eligibility planning checkpoint on 2026-06-24: user confirmed branch ownership must be visible for both Customer and Supplier so each branch can know which counterparties belong to it. Target contract is strict mapping tables, not a single branch field on master rows: `customer_branches` and `supplier_branches` own active branch eligibility, support primary branch, and must be the source of truth for transaction selectors/API validation. No fallback is allowed: unmapped Customer/Supplier must not appear in new branch-bound documents, and API writes must reject rather than treating unmapped rows as all-branch. Docs updated before implementation in target requirements, master Customer/Supplier page flows, WTI/WTO, Purchase/Sales canonical flows, PO Sell, Purchase Bill, Sales Bill, and the implementation tasklist. Next implementation batch should start with additive DB/Prisma migration and data audit/backfill report before tightening runtime selectors.

WTI/WTO impurity option checkpoint on 2026-06-24: user confirmed `สินค้าอื่น` must not come from master impurity data and must not fallback to legacy master rows. Runtime now treats `สินค้าอื่น` as a WTI-only system option with id `__OTHER_PRODUCT__`; the WTI modal injects it from code, filters master rows named `สินค้าอื่น`/`อื่นๆ`/`อย่างอื่น` out of impurity options, and WTO never shows it. Create/update APIs reject WTO payloads that use the system option and reject payloads that try to use master impurity rows for `สินค้าอื่น`; new writes store the special option as system-owned impurity name with no master `impurity_id`. Read runtime also does not translate historical/master `สินค้าอื่น` rows back into the system option; old bad rows require data repair/master deactivation instead of runtime fallback.
WTO pending-out cleanup checkpoint on 2026-06-24: continued removal of the old Pending Sale / PSALE runtime flow after the target decision that stock sale must be `WTO pending_out -> Sales Bill -> SB ledger`. Sales Bill validation no longer exposes `pendingStockIssueId`, `fromPsaleNo`, or `fromPsaleId`; the Sales Bill API no longer has a PSALE payload guard or PSALE cancel/data-repair reject path and now follows the target Sales Bill schema/WTO usage path only. Active dashboard/finance links that previously opened `/sales/stock-issue` now point to `/sales/bills` and use `WTO pending out` wording, Trading Matching flow copy now reads `PO Sell -> WTO -> Sales Bill Trading`, and Stock Ledger no longer links legacy `PSALE` rows to the removed route. The active route file `apps/next/src/app/sales/stock-issue/page.tsx` and API file `apps/next/src/app/api/sales/stock-issue/route.ts` were deleted, so `/sales/stock-issue` and `/api/sales/stock-issue` are no longer active app routes. The shared transaction list component `TransactionBillsPageClient` now accepts only `purchase | sales`; the unreachable `mode="stock-issue"` type/state/API/form/modal/table/action branches were removed from that component.

WTI LINE image UAT repair checkpoint on 2026-07-01: investigated customer UAT reports that sharing a WTI to LINE sent without the expected images. Root cause was environment/storage contract drift: earlier UAT notification logs stored PDF URLs on the dev Supabase host because the UAT deployment still had dev Storage env at send time, and the customer UAT Supabase project did not yet have a usable `weight-ticket-pdfs` bucket. The bucket contract also only allowed `application/pdf` while the current LINE flow uploads PDF, generated album JPEGs, and WTI/WTO source images as PNG/JPEG. Added migration `20260701070000_allow_weight_ticket_line_image_storage.sql`, updated the admin LINE setup helper, applied the bucket repair directly to UAT, and verified public reads for PNG and PDF on `oolzfvqhovmjhiocfqdw.supabase.co`. The business rule remains: WTI/WTO LINE share stores generated PDF and image snapshots in public Supabase Storage so LINE can fetch them without user authentication.
Sales/WTO detail cost snapshot checkpoint on 2026-07-01: fixed detail read models after user found `SB2607-0005` Source usage facts and `WTO012607-0005` detail showing blank cost values. Root cause was read-model-only: Sales Bill detail mapped WTO usage log amount to `0` even though the posted `SB` stock ledger already held COGS, and WTO detail calculated product cost only from `active` stock holds even after a billed WTO consumes the hold. The target flow is unchanged: WTO confirmation locks `stock_holds.unit_cost_snapshot/value_snapshot`; Sales Bill posting writes `SB` stock ledger `value_out`; detail pages must read those durable facts even after pending_out has been consumed. The read model now derives WTO usage COGS from the existing sales line stock COGS/ledger facts and keeps WTO average cost visible from active or consumed hold snapshots without inventing fallback cost.

Stock balance WTO/SB bucket repair on 2026-06-13: investigated user-reported `/stock/balance` mismatch for `POS6906-0001` / `SB2606-0001`, where Stock Balance showed `SKU001` as `RM +110` plus a separate `- -5` row instead of `RM 105`. Root cause was not warehouse loss: `WTO012606-0001` stores warehouse at line/hold level (`RM-SK`) and `SB2606-0001` consumes that hold, but the generated `SB` ledger row did not carry `output_category`, so the stock-out aggregated into the `-` bucket. Added migration [supabase/migrations/20260613084801_add_stock_hold_bucket_fields.sql](/Users/watcharathatsrithanesiganon/Documents/GitHub/ns-scrap-erp/supabase/migrations/20260613084801_add_stock_hold_bucket_fields.sql) to add bucket fields to `stock_holds`, backfill existing holds from warehouse type, repair resolvable `SB`/`PSALE` ledger rows consumed from holds, and rebuild the hold lookup index with `output_category`. Runtime now records hold bucket fields when creating WTO holds, validates/allocates from saleable bucket matching the selected warehouse type, and writes `SB`/`PSALE` ledger rows with hold `output_category`, `lot_no`, and `not_available_for_sale`. Dev-target apply verified `SB2606-0001` now has `output_category = RM` and `SKU001 / RM-SK / RM` aggregates to `105` kg. Validation passed: Prisma generate/validate, `type-check`, `verify:stock-ledger` with `.env.local`, `lint` with only the existing Products `<img>` warning, `build`, and `git diff --check`.

Runtime PSALE/production stock-ledger service QA checkpoint on 2026-06-12: `apps/next/scripts/verify-stock-ledger-contract.ts` now gates both stock and production reconciliation. In addition to the stock reconciliation groups, it fails on production reconciliation issues, reversed `PI`/`PO2` rows whose `PI-REV`/`PO2-REV` ledger rows are missing or do not net back to zero, and duplicate production reversal document numbers reused across different source docs. New `npm run qa:stock-ledger-write-paths --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next` adds repeatable dev-target write-path QA without hardcoded branch/product/warehouse master codes: it resolves a valid production scenario from current stock/master data, creates and cancels a PSALE from an active WTO hold, creates PI/PO2 production movement, reverses PO2 then PI, and verifies reconciliation remains clean. The first repeated service QA exposed a production doc-number bug: `PI-REV`/`PO2-REV` generation scanned `doc_no` even though reversal numbers are stored in `reversal_doc_no`, so repeated reversals could reuse `...0001`. Runtime generation now scans `reversal_doc_no` for `*-REV` prefixes, and migration [supabase/migrations/20260612233500_repair_duplicate_production_reversal_doc_numbers.sql](/Users/watcharathatsrithanesiganon/Documents/GitHub/ns-scrap-erp/supabase/migrations/20260612233500_repair_duplicate_production_reversal_doc_numbers.sql) generically renumbers duplicate dev-target reversal groups and updates matching `stock_ledger.ref_no` plus production status-log metadata. The migration was applied directly to dev-target and marked in `supabase_migrations.schema_migrations`. Final service QA after the fix passed: `PSALE2606-0006` from `WTO012606-0005` wrote `PSALE` + `PSALE-CANCEL` net zero and reopened the hold; production QA created `PO2606-0024`, `PI2606-0023`, `PO22606-0008`, `PO2-REV2606-0003`, and `PI-REV2606-0003` with all expected `PI/PI-REV/PO2/PO2-REV` ledger ref types present. `npm run verify:stock-ledger` then returned all stock totals `0` and production `issueCount = 0`. Production build passed. Browser QA was attempted against `http://127.0.0.1:3005`, but the Playwright transport closed before navigation; unauthenticated HTTP smoke confirmed `/stock/reconciliation`, `/production/reconciliation`, and `/sales/stock-issue` redirect to login as expected. Remaining stock-ledger runtime follow-up is logged-in browser QA evidence for PSALE UI convert/cancel and any required UI rerun for the exact production write-path batch; PSALE edit remains policy-open and should stay cancel/recreate unless product explicitly requires in-place edit semantics.
PSALE edit policy update on 2026-06-12: user confirmed PSALE can be edited while it has not been pulled into another document. The implemented policy is now: edit only when `stock_issues.status = pending` and `converted_to_bill_id` is empty; keep the same PSALE doc no and WTO source; changing WTO source requires cancel/recreate. `/api/sales/stock-issue` now supports `PATCH action = edit`: it reverses only currently unreversed `PSALE` ledger rows with appended `PSALE-CANCEL`, reopens the WTO hold, consumes it again under the same PSALE doc no, updates item/date/note/estimated amount snapshots, and appends `stock_issue_status_logs.action = edited`. `/sales/stock-issue` UI now enables the edit button for pending PSALE only, opens the existing form with row snapshot values, locks the WTO selector during edit, and submits `PATCH action = edit`. Service QA now covers create -> edit -> cancel for PSALE; the latest dev-target run created `PSALE2606-0007`, edited it append-only, cancelled it, and `npm run verify:stock-ledger` returned all stock totals `0` with production `issueCount = 0`. The edit policy is explicit cancel-and-reissue, not silent in-place mutation: submitting an existing RCP from the UI or `PATCH /api/sales/receipts` with `action = replace` cancels the old RCP, writes the reversing `RCP-CANCEL` bank statement and AR/SB restoration, validates replacement lines against restored SB balances, then creates a new RCP in the same transaction with status logs linking the replacement to the old doc no. Runtime weight-ticket options contract checkpoint on 2026-06-11: `/daily/weight-tickets` must not load master product option data through `/api/master-data/products?all=1` because that route returns full product image payloads for the product master page. The target contract is now page-scoped: `/api/daily/weight-tickets/options` returns lightweight header options (branch/supplier/customer/impurity) under the WTI/WTO permission flow, then `/api/daily/weight-tickets/products` preloads product choices in the background immediately after options succeed, without waiting for the user to choose header fields. That same `/products` route now returns the product thumbnail inline with each product row, so the client no longer makes a separate image request. The product picker can load and show product images before branch and supplier/customer are chosen; branch + party are still required by validation before save so the weighing document remains tied to the correct business context. This keeps the user-required product pictures without calling the heavy master product list on page bootstrap. Follow-up remains to move product images from DB/base64 into Storage with generated thumbnail URLs.
Runtime product-image storage checkpoint on 2026-06-11: `/master-data/products` and the shared WTI/WTO product picker now cut over to `products.image_storage_key` with no runtime fallback to old `products.image_names`. Migration `20260611050202_add_product_storage_image_key.sql` was applied directly to `dev-target`; it adds `products.image_storage_key`, creates public bucket `product-images`, and adds authenticated insert/update/delete policies on `storage.objects`. The product modal now saves master-data fields first, uploads the selected image to Storage through the browser-authenticated Supabase client, then persists the storage key back to the product row and best-effort removes the replaced file. `/api/master-data/products` and `/api/daily/weight-tickets/products` now emit `thumbnailUrl` derived from the storage key, so both WTI and WTO product pickers read the same image contract without a separate image API. Validation passed with `npm run prisma:generate --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`, `npm run type-check --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next -- --pretty false`, `npm run lint --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`, `npm run build --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`, and `git diff --check`. Remaining follow-up is cleanup/removal of legacy `products.image_names` data.
Runtime product-image original+thumb checkpoint on 2026-06-11: the product-image flow was hardened from `original only + runtime transform` to explicit `original + thumbnail` objects in Storage. Migration `20260611052713_add_product_image_thumbnail_storage_key.sql` was applied directly to `dev-target`; it adds `products.image_thumbnail_storage_key` beside `image_storage_key`. The product modal now resizes/compresses the selected image in the browser into two `.webp` files before upload: optimized original (`max 1600px`) and thumbnail (`320x320`). Both files are uploaded to `product-images`, then both storage keys are persisted on the product row; if upload/save fails after partial upload, the newly uploaded files are removed best-effort to avoid new orphans. `/api/master-data/products` and `/api/daily/weight-tickets/products` now serve `thumbnailUrl` from the stored thumb object directly instead of runtime transform, so WTI and WTO product pickers read the physical thumbnail file.
Runtime legacy product-image backfill checkpoint on 2026-06-11: legacy `products.image_names` rows were backfilled into the new Storage contract using one-off script [apps/next/scripts/backfill-product-images.mjs](/Users/watcharathatsrithanesiganon/Documents/GitHub/ns-scrap-erp/apps/next/scripts/backfill-product-images.mjs). The script decoded the first legacy image payload per product, generated optimized original + thumbnail files locally with `sips`, uploaded both to bucket `product-images` through `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`, and updated `products.image_storage_key` / `products.image_thumbnail_storage_key` for 62 products with `success=62, failed=0`. On this macOS host, `sips` could not write `webp`, so the backfilled files were written as `jpeg`; runtime does not depend on file extension and continues to read thumb URLs from stored keys normally. Legacy `image_names` source data was intentionally retained for now; cleanup/removal stays as a separate follow-up after user verification.

The same note now also separates `document status` from `mutability/lock state`, and defines `WTO` stock reverse rules for edit/cancel (`edit = reverse + rebuild`, `cancel = reverse only`, both blocked once used in SB). Docs checkpoint on 2026-06-11: aging/date semantics were refined further. `created_at` / system-created timestamp must be visible on every record/document list/detail page as `วันที่สร้างรายการ` for audit, but it must stay separate from business dates such as document date, payment/receipt date, due date, and downstream used date. Backdated documents must keep both business close date and system close timestamp so business aging and process latency do not get mixed.
Docs checkpoint on 2026-06-11: purchase-to-payment status boundaries were normalized across [docs/notes/WTI-WTO Flow.md](/Users/watcharathatsrithanesiganon/Documents/GitHub/ns-scrap-erp/docs/notes/WTI-WTO%20Flow.md), [docs/notes/Purchase Flow.md](/Users/watcharathatsrithanesiganon/Documents/GitHub/ns-scrap-erp/docs/notes/Purchase%20Flow.md), [docs/notes/Purchase Flow Status Matrix.md](/Users/watcharathatsrithanesiganon/Documents/GitHub/ns-scrap-erp/docs/notes/Purchase%20Flow%20Status%20Matrix.md), [docs/notes/Purchase Bills Page Flow.md](/Users/watcharathatsrithanesiganon/Documents/GitHub/ns-scrap-erp/docs/notes/Purchase%20Bills%20Page%20Flow.md), and [docs/notes/Payment Flow.md](/Users/watcharathatsrithanesiganon/Documents/GitHub/ns-scrap-erp/docs/notes/Payment%20Flow.md). Canonical set: `POB` can have partial statuses, `WTI` has only `รับของแล้ว / เสร็จสิ้น / ยกเลิก`, `PB` list/filter uses `ยังไม่อนุมัติ / รอจ่าย / ชำระบางส่วน / เสร็จสิ้น / ยกเลิก`, `PMA` owns `อนุมัติแล้ว / ยกเลิกแล้ว`, and `PMT` owns `เสร็จสิ้น / ยกเลิกแล้ว` while history UI may label them as `จ่ายแล้ว / ยกเลิก`. Lock/edit/cancel remains fact-derived from active WTI/PB/PMA/PMT usage, not status string alone.
Docs checkpoint on 2026-06-11: remaining implementation gaps after the status decision are now tracked explicitly. WTI/WTO still need `WTO` stock hold/reservation, `SB Stock` consume-hold + `stock_ledger.ref_type = SB`, `WTO -> SB` usage/status logs, canonical label cleanup across list/detail/filter/print, and aging/reconciliation reports for legacy partial/status mismatch rows. `/purchase/bills` still needs runtime verification that PB filters use `ยังไม่อนุมัติ / รอจ่าย / ชำระบางส่วน / เสร็จสิ้น / ยกเลิก`, Stock PB selects only `WTI = รับของแล้ว`, and edit/cancel/supplier-swap lock when active `PMA approved` or `PMT active` exists. These are implementation tasks, not new business decisions.
Docs checkpoint on 2026-06-11: WTI/WTO target decisions were confirmed, then superseded by the bill-driven + stock hold legacy alignment later the same day. Final target for this checkpoint is: `WTI save` does not write stock ledger, `WTO save` creates active pending_out but does not write stock ledger, `PB Stock save = stock in`, `SB Stock save = consume hold + stock out`; edit/cancel stock reverse belongs to `PB/SB`, while WTO edit/cancel before billing rebuilds/releases hold; `WTI/WTO` lock after downstream usage. `WTI 1 ใบ -> PB 1 ใบ` and `WTO 1 ใบ -> SB 1 ใบ` remain target rules with no target partial-billed state. WTO UX remains product-first: user selects product in each line first, then selects an active branch-matched `RM/FG` warehouse for that line, after which stock balance is shown as `คงเหลือจริง / จองไว้ / พร้อมส่ง`.

Trading/no-receipt rows still use the PB line note because there is no source receipt note.
Runtime purchase-bill print totals follow-up on 2026-06-10: PB print summary now follows the user-defined order: subtotal, discount, after-discount total, VAT from after-discount total, separator, grand total, deposit/partial-payment deduction, and payable balance. The deposit/partial-payment line uses `paidAmount` so it represents both ADV/mัดจำ and any partial PMT settlement, not just active ADV allocation.
Runtime purchase-bill short-item print follow-up on 2026-06-10: PB print now keeps filler table rows visible in print and extends short bills to a 15-row item table so documents with few products visually stretch toward the footer/signature area. Multi-page PB prints also add filler rows on the final item-table page using a continuation-page capacity of 24 rows, so cases where the last page has only one or a few real item rows still stretch the table toward the footer instead of leaving a mostly empty final page.
Runtime purchase-bill print design checkpoint on 2026-06-09: legacy purchase bills already support per-row printing via `erp.printDocument('receipt', row.raw.id)` (`old-apps/legacy/index.html:15119`) and a popup print helper (`old-apps/legacy/index.html:6449`). Active Next `/purchase/bills` still needs a real per-document PB print action from list/detail/direct detail. Target print must use `/admin/company-profile` / `ข้อมูลบริษัท (สำหรับใบพิมพ์)` as the canonical header source, not hardcoded company data. The customer sample image received on 2026-06-09 is a landscape `ใบรับสินค้า` with delivery/time/seller/truck/preparer/Sale fields, a total-summary band, seller/date/document-number metadata row, and an item table with `สินค้า`, `REMARK`, `นน.ก่อนหัก`, `นน.หัก`, `นน.สุทธิ`, `ราคา`, `รวม`. User clarified after sharing the image that the active app may redesign the form as long as the data is complete and the output looks corporate, so the image is now a data completeness checklist rather than a layout to copy. Required print content and the corporate layout direction are documented in `docs/notes/Purchase Bills Page Flow.md`: PB number/date, Supplier, branch/warehouse, Stock/Trading, line-level PO/Spot source, product rows with actual units (`กก.`/`ลัง`), subtotal/discount/VAT/net/ADV/payable balance, payment status, remarks/reference numbers, and signature lines. This is a PB document print only; it must not create PMA/PMT/BST or any transaction side effect.
Runtime quantity-unit display decision on 2026-06-09: user clarified the target rule for product quantities with units `กก.` and `ลัง`. The active convention is to separate units clearly wherever possible instead of summing different units into one number. Line-item surfaces must show the actual unit from document snapshot or product master, especially PO/PB/SB details, receipt vouchers, print previews, exports, and external-facing documents. Summary/KPI/report surfaces should show grouped totals such as `รวม 1,250 กก. / 32 ลัง` when multiple units exist; only use a single combined quantity if a specific approved conversion rule exists for that report. Internal input labels may use neutral wording like `จำนวน (กก./ลัง)` or `ราคา/หน่วย`, but hardcoded `กก.` is not acceptable for fields that can contain `ลัง`.
Runtime petty-advance modal/design follow-up on 2026-06-09: `/daily/petty-advance` create/edit modal now hides server-owned `PADV` numbers, uses `วันที่จ่าย` as the only user-editable date, removes the old company-account section, and splits the form into compact sections. `ผู้รับเงิน` is now a SearchCombobox backed by active `director_employees` rows of type `กรรมการ` or `พนักงาน` that have receiving bank data; the selected person's receiving account is shown read-only from master data. `petty_advances` now stores recipient person code plus receiving-account snapshots (`recipient_bank_name`, `recipient_bank_account_name`, `recipient_account_no`, `recipient_bank_branch`) so history does not drift when master data changes. `PADV` is now treated as the loan/advance outstanding document only: create/edit no longer creates or rewrites `BST` bank statement rows and no longer requires a company payment account. `BST` is created only when saving a `PRET` return-money entry. The list filter uses segmented filters with `ประเภท` and `สถานะ` on separate rows, table wording uses `วันที่จ่าย`, row click opens detail, both row action and detail modal expose `คืนเงิน` for active rows with remaining amount, notes are textarea, and the money fields use text+decimal input rather than native number. Migration `20260609073126_add_petty_advance_recipient_account_snapshot.sql` was applied to dev-target and marked applied with `supabase migration repair 20260609073126 --status applied`.
Runtime EXP direct-payment checkpoint on 2026-06-09: `/daily/expense` modal now has an explicit mode choice before save: `ส่งอนุมัติ` keeps the existing EXP -> PMA -> PMT path, while `จ่ายเลย` requires Supplier receiving channel, company payment account, Discount, and Bank fee, then creates `EXP` + `PMT` in one transaction without creating `PMA`. Direct EXP PMT writes `payments.lines` source snapshots (`sourceType = expense`, `sourceDocNo = EXP...`), `bank_statement`, `payment_account_splits`, and `payment_status_logs`, so it appears in `/purchase/payments?tab=history` even without `payment_allocations`. Cancelling a direct EXP PMT cancels the PMT/payment facts and sets the source EXP to `cancelled` because there is no PMA to return to the waiting-payment queue. The modal order now asks `วิธีดำเนินการ` first, places Supplier receiving channel after `ผู้รับเงิน`, places `วิธีการจ่าย` after expense lines, filters company payment accounts by payment method from `/master-data/payment-methods`, hides Bank fee for cash methods, and uses a redesigned `สรุปก่อนบันทึก` that separates EXP totals from actual cash-out totals. The expense list row click now opens an in-page detail modal instead of navigating away, the modal follows the compact detail/read-only design with summary cards and expense-line table, and the list table supports sortable resizable headers using the shared `ResizableTableHead` pattern. `docs/notes/Payment Flow.md`, `docs/notes/Daily Cash Flow.md`, and `REQUIREMENTS_TARGET_SYSTEM.md` now describe the same two-mode rule.
Runtime supplier master design follow-up on 2026-06-09: `/master-data/suppliers` list UI now follows `docs/design.md` list/table baseline. The filter card uses `h-9` controls, clear-filter action only when filters are active, lucide icons for Import/Export/Add, and a segmented `สถานะ:` filter (`ทั้งหมด`, `ใช้งาน`, `ปิด`). The table is now a lined/resizable table with shared `ResizableTableHead`, `useResizableColumns('master-data.suppliers')`, persisted column widths, `colgroup` + `table-layout: fixed`, compact `text-xs font-semibold` body cells, slate row dividers, neutral outline row action, visible active toggle labels, and `Set col to default` when widths are customized. Supplier export/list APIs accept the same `active=active|inactive` filter so Excel output matches the visible status filter. Validation passed with `npm run type-check --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next -- --pretty false`, `npm run lint --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`, `npm run build --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`, and `git diff --check`.
Runtime EXP supplier-reference/payment-approval follow-up on 2026-06-09: `/daily/expense` now treats `ผู้รับเงิน` as a required active Supplier master selection and stores the canonical relation in `expenses.supplier_id`; `expenses.payee` remains only a supplier-name snapshot/display value. New migration `20260609061848_add_expenses_supplier_reference.sql` was applied to dev-target and migration history was recorded; it adds the FK/index and backfills old rows only when the normalized `payee` name matches exactly one active supplier, leaving ambiguous rows for data repair instead of adding runtime name resolve. `/daily/payment-approval` now builds EXP `ช่องทางจ่าย / บัญชีปลายทาง` from `expense.suppliers.supplier_bank_accounts` directly, the same model as PB/ADV. The API no longer injects synthetic payment-method options from master data or company cash/bank accounts, and EXP no longer resolves supplier from `expenses.payee` at approval time. A selectable option must come from `supplier_bank_accounts` of that source supplier and may represent either a supplier-specific payment method (for example cash/channel row) or a supplier bank account; labels show payment method, bank name, and account number when present. Supplier export also accepts the active filter used by the page.
Runtime director/company-person master checkpoint on 2026-06-09: `/master-data/directors` is now the company-person master instead of a narrow director/employee-only form. The DB keeps internal `director_employees.id` as bigint autoincrement; the user-facing business code is server-generated text `P001`, `P002`, ... and is hidden from the modal. The modal now sections fields into `ข้อมูลบุคคล` and `ข้อมูลบัญชีรับเงิน`; required fields are `ประเภท`, `คำนำหน้าชื่อ`, `ชื่อ`, and `นามสกุล`, with type options limited to `กรรมการ`, `ผู้ถือหุ้น`, `พนักงาน`, and `บุคคลที่เกี่ยวข้อง`. Phone was removed from the UI. Bank fields are `ธนาคาร`, `ชื่อบัญชี`, `เลขบัญชี`, and `สาขา`; if any bank field is entered, API/client validation requires bank, account name, and digit-only account number. The shared master-data table now uses the lined table baseline with compact font, sortable/resizable headers, persisted column widths, and the active toggle remains visible in status cells. Dev-target `director_employees` was cleared and reseeded with 10 mock rows `P001`-`P010`; no old transaction data was involved. The shared `useResizableColumns(tableKey, columns)` hook persists per-table widths to `localStorage`, requires default/min widths, supports reset to defaults, and keeps resize handles from triggering sort/click actions. The supplier-swap history table was the first consumer: its wide report table uses `colgroup`, `table-layout: fixed`, persisted column widths, a slim header resize handle, horizontal overflow for narrow screens, and a `Set col to default` action when custom widths exist. The section sorts status and allocation events by one timestamp stream but renders latest-first, showing actor, action, transition/source PB, allocation qty/amount/before-after remaining, note/meta, and a latest status marker so the PO lifecycle is read as one sequence instead of separate surfaces. PO Buy status display in both the table and modal now follows the `/purchase/bills` pattern: `dot + สีข้อความ` instead of a filled badge, with clearer semantic colors for open/partial/received/short-closed/cancelled states.
Runtime PB supplier-swap historical source-display follow-up on 2026-06-08: `/purchase/bills/{docNo}` detail now distinguishes active allocation facts from historical source display. For supplier-swap/cancelled PB rows such as `PB012606-0008`, `purchase_bill_po_allocations` may be released/deleted to restore PO remaining, but the detail page must still display the original PO source from `purchase_bill_items.po_buy_id` or `source_snapshot.poBuyId` instead of falling back to `Spot Buy`. `docs/notes/Purchase Bills Page Flow.md` now records this contract explicitly.
Runtime PB supplier-swap cancel-status follow-up on 2026-06-08: when `/purchase/bills` supplier swap saves, the old PB is no longer stored as plain `cancelled`; it uses raw status `cancelled_supplier_swap` and displays `ยกเลิก/เปลี่ยน Supplier`. The status remains treated as a cancelled PB by WTI allocation usage, payment approval/AP queues, cash-position, tracking, and main sales-control read models. New migration `20260608114500_add_purchase_bill_supplier_swap_cancel_status.sql` expands `purchase_bills_status_chk` to allow the status.
Runtime PB supplier-swap ADV lookup follow-up on 2026-06-08: in `/purchase/bills` supplier swap mode, the ADV/มัดจำ search now uses the draft `Supplier ใหม่` instead of the old locked PB supplier. Changing `Supplier ใหม่` clears the selected ADV so an ADV from the previous supplier cannot be carried into the new PB payload. The WTI and original PB supplier remain locked and are not used for the ADV lookup while swap mode is active.
Runtime ADV partially-paid status checkpoint on 2026-06-08: `/purchase/advance-payments` now adds runtime status `partially_paid` (`จ่ายแล้วบางส่วน`) and relabels `paid` as `จ่ายแล้ว`. ADV status priority is `cancelled` > allocation (`allocated` / `partially_allocated`) > payment (`paid` / `partially_paid`) > approval (`approved` / `partially_approved`) > `pending_approval`. Allocation release paths, including PB cancel and supplier swap voiding the old PB, now recalc ADV from active allocation plus actual PMT settlement so an ADV returns from `ใช้หักบิล...` to `จ่ายแล้ว` or `จ่ายแล้วบางส่วน` as appropriate. New migration `20260608113000_add_supplier_advance_partially_paid_status.sql` expands the DB status constraint and backfills current ADV statuses from active PMA/PMT/allocation facts; it was applied to dev-target via direct `psql` and marked applied with `supabase migration repair 20260608113000 --status applied`. DB verification now shows `paid = 1`, `partially_paid = 1`, and the live constraint includes `partially_paid`. Validation passed with `npm run type-check --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`, `npm run lint --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`, `npm run build --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`, `npm run --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next prisma:generate`, and `git diff --check`.
Runtime ADV net-weight input follow-up on 2026-06-08: `/purchase/advance-payments` now derives `น้ำหนักสุทธิ` in the form from `น้ำหนักเข้า - น้ำหนักออก`, shows the net field as read-only, uses the derived value for the summary calculation, and normalizes `netWeight` from the same inputs before submit so the payload matches the displayed value.
Runtime purchase-bill supplier-swap draft-supplier follow-up on 2026-06-08: `/purchase/bills` supplier swap mode no longer unlocks or mutates the original `form.supplierId` while the edit modal is open. The modal now shows Supplier เดิม as readonly, adds a separate `Supplier ใหม่` combobox backed by draft state, and only substitutes that draft supplier into the `supplier_swap` save payload. This removes the remaining post-select/blur reset path where Supplier combobox state could update the main PB form context and cascade into WTI/receipt-dependent UI.
Runtime purchase-bill supplier-swap supplier-blur follow-up on 2026-06-08: `/purchase/bills` supplier swap mode now ignores empty intermediate Supplier values emitted by the supplier search combobox while typing or blurring, so clicking blank space in the modal after choosing a new Supplier cannot push `supplierId = ''` through the normal form-change path. The edit modal also snapshots the original WTI receipt when opening the PB edit flow and reuses that locked receipt snapshot while supplier swap is active, keeping the original receipt visible even if live receipt options are filtered by the newly selected Supplier.
Runtime purchase-bill supplier-swap receipt-lock follow-up on 2026-06-08: `/purchase/bills` supplier swap mode now keeps the original WTI visible after choosing a new Supplier by retaining the selected locked receipt in the combobox option set even when the normal receipt list filters by the new Supplier. The `เปลี่ยน Supplier` button is hidden after entering swap mode, and the `ล้างใบรับของ` button is hidden in edit/supplier-swap contexts so the locked receipt cannot be cleared from this flow. `docs/notes/Purchase Bills Page Flow.md` now records that Supplier changes in swap mode must not reset, clear, or hide the original WTI.
Runtime purchase-bill supplier-swap checkpoint on 2026-06-08: `/purchase/bills` now has a page-specific flow doc at `docs/notes/Purchase Bills Page Flow.md` and an implemented supplier-swap path in the edit modal. The `เปลี่ยน Supplier` button appears beside Supplier only while editing a locked Stock PB with WTI selected; entering the mode keeps branch, warehouse, WTI, row count, source summary, and qty locked, clears old ADV/PO selection, and forces all new lines to `Spot Buy เท่านั้น`. `PATCH /api/purchase/bills` action `supplier_swap` validates no active PMA/PMT, requires the original WTI source, rejects any PO allocation, rejects changed rows/source/qty, voids the old PB with stock/WTI/PO/ADV release side effects, creates a replacement PB with a new `PB...` number, writes new stock ledger for the replacement bill, and creates `bill_swap_history` rows linked to the old PB with the replacement PB doc no in `reason`. ADV allocation from the old PB is released and is not carried to the new PB. Validation passed with `npm run type-check --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`, `npm run lint --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`, `npm run build --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`, and `git diff --check`. Headless mobile smoke on `http://127.0.0.1:3000/purchase/bills` redirected unauthenticated to `/login?redirect=%2Fpurchase%2Fbills`, reported `overflow = 0`, and had no HTTP responses `>= 400`; the only console error was the local dev HMR websocket handshake noise.
Runtime expense docs/flow sync on 2026-06-08: target requirements and Payment Flow now document `EXP` as the expense source document for approval/payment lifecycle. Runtime daily transfer modal/design checkpoint on 2026-06-08: `/daily/transfer` modal now hides system-managed fields from user entry. `เลขที่` is no longer shown in the modal, `วันที่` stays auto-filled by the client/server write path instead of being edited in the modal, and `ผู้ทำรายการ` remains the authenticated creator from `created_by` rather than a form field. Runtime daily transfer save 400 follow-up on 2026-06-08: `/api/daily/transfers` POST save could fail in the local/dev runtime because new `TRF` and paired `BST` doc numbers were generated inside `prisma.$transaction` through the global Prisma client instead of the active transaction client. This matched the same constrained-pool transaction pattern already fixed in PO short-close and expenses. Transfer save now calls `nextDailyDocNo('transfers', 'TRF', date, tx)` and `nextDailyDocNos('bank_statement', 'BST', date, 2, tx)` so document numbering, transfer insert/update, old statement cleanup, and paired bank-statement posting stay on the same transaction connection.

The note is the current canonical page flow for transfer UX and bank-statement side effects until a broader cash/bank flow document supersedes it.
Runtime daily transfer row-detail follow-up on 2026-06-08: `/daily/transfer` table rows are now clickable and keyboard-openable to a detail modal that summarizes the selected `TRF`, transfer amount, fee, source/destination accounts, note, actor, and the paired Bank Statement impact. Row action clicks stop propagation so `แก้ไข` opens edit directly instead of opening detail first. The disabled destructive action label is now `ยกเลิก` instead of `ลบ`, pending a reviewed append-only transfer reversal flow.
Runtime expense list detail navigation follow-up on 2026-06-08: `/daily/expense` list now labels the row date column as `วันที่จ่าย`, and table rows are clickable to open `/daily/expense/{docNo}` detail pages. Row-level `แก้ไข` / `ยกเลิก` actions stop propagation so they keep their existing modal/cancel behavior instead of navigating.
Runtime expense payment-date follow-up on 2026-06-08: `/daily/expense` create/edit modal now exposes required `วันที่จ่าย` using the shared date picker and existing `expenseFormSchema.date` validation. `/api/daily/expenses` now uses the submitted `date` for `expenses.date`; new `EXP` running numbers still remain server-owned but their year/month sequence is based on the selected payment date.
Runtime expense category searchable follow-up on 2026-06-08: `/daily/expense` create/edit line-item `หมวดค่าใช้จ่าย` now uses the shared `SearchCombobox` instead of a plain row select. Users can type-search category name, category code, or expense type text inside the modal table, while the save payload still submits the same optional `lines[].categoryId` value and keeps the existing expense write contract unchanged.
Runtime expense-dashboard legacy-function follow-up on 2026-06-09: `/daily/expense-dashboard` now ports the legacy `view-expenseDashboard` calculation function into the active Next client. The dashboard again builds active category buckets plus `_uncat`, uses header-level `row.categoryId`, sums `row.amount + row.vat` per expense/month, sorts categories by total, computes `avg/latest/prev/vsAvg/deviation`, and applies the legacy anomaly rules (`high` when latest exceeds both `1.5× avg` and 5,000; `low` when latest is positive but below `30% avg`). Legacy dashboard wording/icons for period selector, KPI labels, anomaly cards, status pills, and rule note were restored while keeping the topbar-driven page title. `docs/notes/Expense Dashboard Flow.md` is now the page-specific flow doc for this read-only dashboard contract and is indexed in `docs/migration/00-doc-index.md`.
Runtime Thai business-date helper follow-up on 2026-06-09: `todayDateInput()` now returns the current `YYYY-MM-DD` using `Asia/Bangkok` instead of slicing UTC `toISOString()`. This makes `/daily/expense-dashboard` year/month rollover follow Thai business date and also affects daily/finance/stock form defaults that import the same helper, such as payment date, transfer date, due date, and default report filters. Export filenames and utilities that still call `new Date().toISOString()` directly are intentionally outside this helper change. `docs/notes/Expense Dashboard Flow.md` now records the dashboard-specific date/year rollover behavior and helper impact.
Runtime PO Sell flow-doc checkpoint on 2026-06-09: `docs/notes/PO Sell Flow.md` now captures the page-specific `/sales/po-sell` contract after the legacy comparison. New PO Sell rows start as raw `Open` and derived `Not Matched`, should appear immediately in the PO Sell table, and should feed downstream read models including `/dual-costing/cost-allocator`, `/po-reports/outstanding`, and `/sales/bills` / `/sales/stock-issue` handoff. The doc also records current gaps before coding: branch-aware POS numbering, Thai PO Sell lifecycle statuses, line-level PO Sell allocation in sales bills, and stock-issue integration.
Runtime PO Sell downstream integration checkpoint on 2026-06-09: `/sales/po-sell` now separates normalized document status (`เปิดอยู่`, `ยกเลิก`, `ปิดแล้ว`) from match status in both filters and table display, and the match filter includes `Cancelled`. `GET /api/sales/po-sell` normalizes raw `Cancelled/cancelled/Canceled/canceled`, `Completed/Closed`, and zero remaining quantity into stable document-status values instead of exposing raw status as the only filter. `POST /api/sales/bills` now consumes selected bill-level `poSellId`: it validates active PO Sell, customer, branch, product codes, and remaining quantity; creates the sales bill and updates `po_sells.items[].remainingQty`, `remaining_qty`, `remaining_amount`, `cut_amount`, and final `Completed` status in one transaction. `/po-reports/outstanding` and `/dual-costing/cost-allocator` now exclude closed/completed/cancelled/canceled PO Sell rows from active downstream lists. Line-level PO Sell allocation and stock-issue/PSALE integration remain follow-up scope.

The `ผู้รับเงิน` search datalist is now restricted to active Supplier master rows only; Customer, Sale, and employee sources are no longer returned as payee suggestions. Runtime expense save 400 follow-up on 2026-06-08: `/daily/expense` POST save could fail after the transaction-data cleanup because the create path generated the new `EXP` doc no inside `prisma.$transaction` while calling `nextDailyDocNo()` through the global Prisma client. This repeats the single-connection transaction deadlock pattern already seen in PO short-close when the local/dev runtime pool is constrained. `/api/daily/expenses` now takes an advisory transaction lock on `expenses.doc_no` for new rows and calls `nextDailyDocNo('expenses', 'EXP', date, tx)` through the same transaction client, keeping doc-number generation and insert on one connection.

Runtime DB connection checkpoint on 2026-06-07: `/api/auth/me`, `/api/activity`, and `/api/master-data/impurities` reported shared `500` failures while Supabase session pooler returned `EMAXCONNSESSION max clients reached in session mode`. This was not an impurity-table schema issue. `apps/next/src/lib/server/prisma.ts` now resolves runtime DB URLs from `DATABASE_RUNTIME_URL` / `DATABASE_PRISMA_URL` / `DATABASE_URL` and normalizes Supabase pooler URLs from session port `5432` to transaction-pooler port `6543` before creating the shared `pg` pool. It also recreates the pool/client if the runtime URL changes, keeping local/Vercel from holding stale session-pooler connections after env or HMR changes. Runtime PO Buy allocation-key checkpoint on 2026-06-07: `POB012605-0005` exposed a stale-reconciliation bug in the purchase-bill PO allocation flow. The DB still showed `po_buys.status = Open` and `remaining_qty = 120`, while active `purchase_bill_po_allocations` already consumed `240` kg through `PB012605-0420`, `PB012605-0421`, and `PB012606-0010`. Root cause was not a UI selector issue: old `po_buys.items` rows stored product keys as business codes such as `SKU001`, while `purchase_bill_po_allocations.purchase_bill_items.product_id` stores canonical internal bigint ids such as `3`; `reconcilePoBuys()` compared these mismatched keys and therefore did not reduce remaining qty/status. Migration `20260607111513_normalize_po_buy_item_product_keys.sql` now backfills resolvable `po_buys.items.productIdInternal` from current `products.code` without guessing legacy `P###` values, and dev-target migration history was repaired as applied. `reconcilePoBuys()` now requires canonical internal product ids for JSON item rows instead of falling back to `productId`/code, persists `productIdInternal` back into item snapshots, and `/api/purchase/bills` validates PO remaining qty by `PO + product` rather than header-level remaining qty. PO options now use the first remaining canonical item for display/filtering; legacy non-canonical PO rows are not offered as active options instead of breaking the page or falling back. Dev-target reconciliation refreshed 2 canonical allocated PO rows. Post-check for `POB012605-0005`: status is `Partially Received`, total qty `120`, `SKU001/productIdInternal=3` remaining `0`, `SKU003/productIdInternal=5` remaining `20`, cut amount `1000`, and remaining amount `600`. Existing over-allocation evidence remains visible in `purchase_bill_po_allocations` (`SKU001` active allocations total `240`) and was not deleted automatically. Validation passed with `npm run type-check --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next -- --pretty false`, `npm run lint --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`, `npm run build --workspace @ns-scrap-erp/next`, and `git diff --check`.

That behavior is no longer current. The active rule as of 2026-06-08 is that `/purchase/bills` auto-selects the active RM warehouse for the selected branch, renders `คลัง` read-only, recalculates it on branch change, hides/clears it for Trading, and rejects missing/inactive/cross-branch/non-RM warehouses in `/api/purchase/bills`. Validation evidence from the older checkpoint remains historical only.

Runtime purchase-bill scope checkpoint on 2026-06-06: the immediate blocker "บันทึกบิลรับซื้อไม่ได้" is fixed in `/api/purchase/bills`. The stock PB write contract now treats `item.productId` as outward `products.code` only, resolves it once to internal `products.id`, and validates WTI receipt summaries by that resolved internal id without reparsing or falling back to legacy/internal ids. A follow-up UI save bug was also fixed: `/purchase/bills` options expose `receiptTicketId = weight_tickets.doc_no`, summary ids as `${doc_no}:${productCode}:${lineCount}`, and line ids as `${doc_no}:${line_no}`, so the API now resolves those outward keys back to internal bigint ids before writing `purchase_bill_receipt_allocations`; it no longer parses client receipt keys as bigint. Dev-target data cleanup followed the same rule instead of adding code fallback: 4 old test `purchase_bill_items.source_snapshot` rows (`PB012606-0001` through `PB012606-0004`) were backfilled from internal WTI/summary/line ids to outward WTI doc/composite keys, and the post-check count for numeric `source_snapshot.receiptTicketId` is now `0`. Live smoke evidence created `POB012606-0010`, `WTI012606-0007`, `PB012606-0005`, and `PB012606-0006`; PO status moved `Partially Received -> Received`, WTI status became `billed`, and both PB rows reached the approval queue. Runtime supplier-payment PMA split checkpoint on 2026-06-06: `/purchase/payments` now treats approved PMA rows as the UI/API selection identity, while the source PB/ADV document remains an explicit reference. Root cause for `PMA012605-0011/2` being unable to save was twofold: the payment queue exposed split PMAs from the same PB with the same row id/source doc key, and the shared daily doc-number schema rejected `/` even though PMA split documents are valid business doc numbers (`.../1`, `.../2`). `/api/purchase/payments` now returns PMA doc no as `id`/`approvalId`, requires `payment_approvals.source_doc_no_snapshot` as the PB/ADV reference instead of falling back to source table doc no, and resolves supplier party ids from either internal bigint id or valid supplier code without falling back to junk display values. The payment modal converts the selected PMA back to `sourceDocNo` only for the POST `billId`, keeps `lines[].approvalId` as the PMA doc no, and initializes single-account split amount in state instead of silently filling it during submit normalization. Browser QA on `localhost:3000/purchase/payments` for `PMA012605-0011/2` verified GET `/api/purchase/payments` = `200`, row supplier/ยอด `1,000.00` correct, modal split total `1,000.00` matches net cash out, and an intercepted POST payload contains `billId = PB012605-0387`, `supplierId = SU0506`, `accountId = AC-MOVBEKA2NLYD`, `lines[0].approvalId = PMA012605-0011/2`, `lines[0].billId = PB012605-0387`, and `splits[0].amount = 1000`. The POST was intentionally aborted by Playwright to avoid creating a real PMT in dev data. Runtime supplier-payment PMT checkpoint on 2026-06-07: the same `PMA012605-0011/2` was pushed through the real PMT write path in dev-target. The remaining POST `500 DATABASE_ERROR` root cause was transaction timeout `P2028`: `/api/purchase/payments` called `nextDailyDocNos('bank_statement', ...)` inside an interactive transaction, but the helper used the global Prisma client instead of the transaction client; with the local pool at `max=1`, generating the `BST` doc no waited on the active transaction until timeout. `nextDailyDocNo()` / `nextDailyDocNos()` now accept an optional Prisma client/transaction and `/api/purchase/payments` passes `tx` for the bank-statement doc numbers. Runtime payment-approval source-derived pending checkpoint on 2026-06-07: `/daily/payment-approval` now treats `ยังไม่อนุมัติ` as source-derived rows from `PB / ADV / EXP`, not `PMA pending`. Migration `20260607014615_remove_pending_payment_approvals.sql` voided the 150 legacy `payment_approvals.status = pending` placeholder rows, added PMA status logs with action `legacy_pending_placeholder_voided`, changed `payment_approvals.status` default to `approved`, and hardened the DB constraint to allow only `approved`, `paid`, and `voided`. POST now accepts source doc no as `approvalId`, looks up the source by `sourceType + doc_no`, and creates new `PMA approved` rows for the submitted split amounts instead of updating a pending PMA row. Dev-target DB and Prisma use `public.impurities.id bigint generated by identity` as the internal FK key and `code` as the business key, but the active API still generated legacy string ids such as `IMP-###` into `id` and omitted `code` from read responses. No fallback to business code or display text was added for FK writes. Runtime PMA/PMT timeline checkpoint on 2026-06-07: PMA/PMT now have dedicated business timeline tables and fact tables. Runtime document timeline policy checkpoint on 2026-06-06: the target architecture now treats every user-facing business document with a document number (`doc_no`, `document_no`, `voucher_no`, or `ref_no`) as requiring timeline/history. [Document Timeline Policy](/Users/watcharathatsrithanesiganon/Documents/GitHub/ns-scrap-erp/docs/notes/Document%20Timeline%20Policy.md) records the rule: current document tables hold latest state, append-only event logs hold history, detail pages must expose timeline/history, event rows need stable `event_key`, and runtime code must not fabricate history from internal ids or fallback around bad data.
Runtime document history design checkpoint on 2026-06-06: the table design is now explicit that NS Scrap ERP should not use one generic `document_events` table as the source of truth for business timeline. [Document History Table Design](/Users/watcharathatsrithanesiganon/Documents/GitHub/ns-scrap-erp/docs/notes/Document%20History%20Table%20Design.md) sets the target: keep status/usage/allocation history separated by document or business flow (`weight_ticket_status_logs`, `weight_ticket_usage_logs`, `po_buy_allocation_logs`, `supplier_advance_status_logs`, `payment_approval_status_logs`, `payment_status_logs`, etc.), keep typed fact tables for enforceable details, and let UI/read services aggregate per-document timeline views. This is docs/design only; no schema migration was applied in this checkpoint.
